# Test source

```ts
  26  | // still fails the build — this allowlist only prevents already-filed
  27  | // issues from re-blocking CI on every run. Remove an entry once the
  28  | // underlying issue is fixed; if a rule shows up on a new route it will
  29  | // fail and surface as a real regression.
  30  | //
  31  | // Third-party widgets (Frigade, Stripe Elements) are known to emit their
  32  | // own violations we can't fix; narrow the scan to first-party content
  33  | // via `exclude`.
  34  | 
  35  | type Route = { path: string; name: string; phi?: boolean };
  36  | 
  37  | // /login is an Auth0-hosted page; its a11y is Auth0's responsibility and
  38  | // authenticated contexts redirect away from it. Scan first-party routes only.
  39  | const ROUTES: Route[] = [
  40  |   { path: '/dashboard/home', name: 'home' },
  41  |   { path: '/dashboard/appointments', name: 'calendar' },
  42  |   { path: '/dashboard/creative-suite', name: 'creative-suite' },
  43  |   { path: '/dashboard/settings/profile', name: 'settings-profile' },
  44  |   { path: '/dashboard/settings/subscription', name: 'settings-subscription' },
  45  |   { path: '/dashboard/settings/note-templates', name: 'settings-note-templates' },
  46  |   { path: '/dashboard/forms', name: 'forms' },
  47  |   { path: '/dashboard/clients', name: 'clients', phi: true },
  48  |   { path: '/dashboard/clinical-notes', name: 'clinical-notes', phi: true },
  49  |   // High-traffic routes added 2026-07-01 (a11y state verified live on staging):
  50  |   //   storybooks / toolkits / billing → 0 critical (billing has 2 serious →
  51  |   //   warn-only). community → 1 known critical (button-name); games → 1 known
  52  |   //   critical (aria-valid-attr-value) — both allowlisted below.
  53  |   // Deliberately NOT added: /dashboard/marketplace (redirects to /home, already
  54  |   //   covered) and /dashboard/in-person-tools (no <h1> + Colyseus-heavy → scan
  55  |   //   timing is unreliable for an unattended sweep).
  56  |   { path: '/dashboard/community', name: 'community' },
  57  |   { path: '/dashboard/storybooks', name: 'storybooks' },
  58  |   { path: '/dashboard/toolkits', name: 'toolkits' },
  59  |   { path: '/dashboard/games', name: 'games' },
  60  |   { path: '/dashboard/billing', name: 'billing' },
  61  | ];
  62  | 
  63  | async function scanPage(page: import('@playwright/test').Page, path: string) {
  64  |   // domcontentloaded avoids the long-lived-connection hangs on /settings/
  65  |   // subscription and /community.
  66  |   await page.goto(path, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });
  67  | 
  68  |   // Wait for the page's main heading to mount before axe runs. Without
  69  |   // this, CI sometimes scans a half-hydrated page where icon-only buttons
  70  |   // haven't received their aria-labels yet — producing flaky button-name
  71  |   // criticals that pass on retry. Locally these never fire because of
  72  |   // warm caches; CI hits them under cold-load timing.
  73  |   // .catch(() => null) covers routes whose H1 lazy-loads after data
  74  |   // (forms / clients tabs) — we still fall through to the timeout buffer.
  75  |   await page
  76  |     .locator('h1, h2[id*="title"], [role="main"] h2')
  77  |     .first()
  78  |     .waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 10_000 })
  79  |     .catch(() => null);
  80  | 
  81  |   // Settle buffer: covers tab content hydration that lands after the H1.
  82  |   // 4s is comfortably above the worst observed CI hydration tail.
  83  |   await page.waitForTimeout(4000);
  84  | 
  85  |   return new AxeBuilder({ page })
  86  |     .withTags(['wcag2a', 'wcag2aa', 'wcag21a', 'wcag21aa'])
  87  |     .exclude('iframe') // 3rd-party widgets
  88  |     .exclude('[data-frigade]')
  89  |     .exclude('[data-stripe]')
  90  |     .analyze();
  91  | }
  92  | 
  93  | // Rules that fire on dashboard *chrome* — same element on every route
  94  | // (header, sidebar, avatar). Pre-filed; suppressed globally so we don't
  95  | // re-list them on each route in KNOWN_CRITICAL.
  96  | //   - image-alt: user-avatar-dropdown <img> has no alt attribute
  97  | const KNOWN_CRITICAL_GLOBAL: Set<string> = new Set(['image-alt']);
  98  | 
  99  | // Path → set of axe rule IDs known to fire only on that specific route.
  100 | // Filed as product issues; suppressed here so they don't re-fail CI.
  101 | const KNOWN_CRITICAL: Record<string, Set<string>> = {
  102 |   '/dashboard/home': new Set(['button-name']),
  103 |   '/dashboard/clients': new Set(['button-name']),
  104 |   '/dashboard/forms': new Set(['button-name']),
  105 |   // Discovered 2026-07-01 when these routes were added to the sweep; filed as
  106 |   // ENG-2701 — remove each entry once fixed upstream. A *new* rule on these
  107 |   // routes still fails the build.
  108 |   '/dashboard/community': new Set(['button-name']),
  109 |   '/dashboard/games': new Set(['aria-valid-attr-value']),
  110 | };
  111 | 
  112 | function partition<T extends { id: string; impact?: string | null }>(violations: T[], path: string) {
  113 |   const known = new Set<string>([
  114 |     ...(KNOWN_CRITICAL[path] ?? new Set<string>()),
  115 |     ...KNOWN_CRITICAL_GLOBAL,
  116 |   ]);
  117 |   const critical = violations.filter((v) => v.impact === 'critical' && !known.has(v.id));
  118 |   const knownCritical = violations.filter((v) => v.impact === 'critical' && known.has(v.id));
  119 |   const warn = violations.filter((v) => v.impact === 'serious' || v.impact === 'moderate' || v.impact === 'minor');
  120 |   return { critical, knownCritical, warn };
  121 | }
  122 | 
  123 | for (const route of ROUTES) {
  124 |   test.describe(`a11y — ${route.name}`, () => {
  125 |     test(`${route.path} has no new critical WCAG violations`, async ({ page }) => {
> 126 |       const results = await scanPage(page, route.path);
      |                       ^ Error: page.evaluate: Test timeout of 30000ms exceeded.
  127 |       const { critical, knownCritical, warn } = partition(results.violations, route.path);
  128 | 
  129 |       for (const v of warn) {
  130 |         test.info().annotations.push({
  131 |           type: `a11y-${v.impact}`,
  132 |           description: `${v.id}: ${v.help} (${v.nodes.length} node${v.nodes.length === 1 ? '' : 's'})`,
  133 |         });
  134 |       }
  135 |       for (const v of knownCritical) {
  136 |         test.info().annotations.push({
  137 |           type: 'a11y-known-critical',
  138 |           description: `${v.id}: ${v.help} (${v.nodes.length} node${v.nodes.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}) — pre-filed`,
  139 |         });
  140 |       }
  141 | 
  142 |       // Always log a one-line summary for traceability, even on pass.
  143 |       console.log(
  144 |         `[a11y] ${route.path}: critical-new=${critical.length}, critical-known=${knownCritical.length}, serious/moderate/minor=${warn.length}`,
  145 |       );
  146 |       // Log the new critical rule IDs alongside the summary so a CI
  147 |       // failure surfaces WHICH rule fired without grepping the error
  148 |       // stack. (The thrown Error below has the same info, but logs are
  149 |       // easier to scan in GitHub Actions output.)
  150 |       for (const v of critical) {
  151 |         console.log(`  • [critical-NEW] ${v.id}: ${v.help} (${v.nodes.length} node${v.nodes.length === 1 ? '' : 's'})`);
  152 |       }
  153 |       for (const v of knownCritical) {
  154 |         console.log(`  • [known-critical] ${v.id}: ${v.help} (${v.nodes.length} node${v.nodes.length === 1 ? '' : 's'})`);
  155 |       }
  156 |       for (const v of warn) {
  157 |         console.log(`  • [${v.impact}] ${v.id}: ${v.help} (${v.nodes.length} node${v.nodes.length === 1 ? '' : 's'})`);
  158 |       }
  159 | 
  160 |       if (critical.length > 0) {
  161 |         const summary = critical
  162 |           .map((v) => `  - [${v.impact}] ${v.id}: ${v.help} (${v.nodes.length} node${v.nodes.length === 1 ? '' : 's'})`)
  163 |           .join('\n');
  164 |         throw new Error(`${critical.length} new critical a11y violation(s) on ${route.path}:\n${summary}`);
  165 |       }
  166 | 
  167 |       expect(critical.length, `zero new critical a11y violations on ${route.path}`).toBe(0);
  168 |     });
  169 |   });
  170 | }
  171 | 
```
